    <div class="toc">
     <h4>
      Android WebView 优化/离线包开发出现Crash： A Fatal signal 5 , code 1, fault addr 0x6e1f33c798 in tid 32217
     </h4>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <ul>
        <li>
         <a href="#_2" rel="nofollow">

    </div>
    <p>
    </p>
    <h3>
     <a id="_2">
     </a>
     一、问题
    </h3>
    <p>
     Android WebView 出现Crash
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-csharp">A  Fatal signal <span class="token number">5</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>SIGTRAP<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> code <span class="token number">1</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>TRAP_BRKPT<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> fault addr <span class="token number">0x6e1f33c798</span> <span class="token keyword">in</span> tid <span class="token number">32217</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>ThreadPoolForeg<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> pid <span class="token number">32154</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>swing<span class="token punctuation">.</span>demo<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h3>
     <a id="_9">
     </a>
     二、分析
    </h3>
    <p>
     初步排查是WebView Chrom内核出现的错误，具体可看
     <a href="https://groups.google.com/d/msgid/google-admob-ads-sdk/3aa2ad26-f54c-46d1-9072-9c829297de9f@googlegroups.com" rel="nofollow">
      https://groups.google.com/d/msgid/google-admob-ads-sdk/3aa2ad26-f54c-46d1-9072-9c829297de9f%40googlegroups.com
     </a>
    </p>
    <p>
     相关博客回复中，需要把log中
     <br/>
     <code>
      -----BEGIN CRASHPAD MINIDUMP----- 到 -----END CRASHPAD MINIDUMP-----
     </code>
     <br/>
     之间的日志发送给WebView Chrom团队地位问题。。。
    </p>
    <p>
     <strong>
      这不应该是WebView Chrom内核的问题，不然得更新系统WebView内核了
     </strong>
    </p>
    <p>
     <strong>
      但是是什么原因导致chromium 出现错误呢？
     </strong>
    </p>
    <p>
     先从代码逻辑入手，目前正在开发的是
    </p>
    <p>
     <em>
      WebView离线包功能，对资源进行拦截，第一次将资源下载到磁盘，今后则使用磁盘资源，达到H5优化的目的。
     </em>
    </p>
    <p>
     <mark>
      果然 当把资源拦截关闭时，不会出现这个Crash了。
     </mark>
    </p>
    <p>
     定位具体是哪种资源拦截的问题？
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      CSS?
     </li>
     <li>
      JS?
     </li>
     <li>
      IMAGE?
     </li>
     <li>
      …?
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     原因是Image
    </p>
    <p>
     调试过程中，日志平台里出现Warn
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-csharp">com<span class="token punctuation">.</span>facebook<span class="token punctuation">.</span>imagepipeline<span class="token punctuation">.</span>memory<span class="token punctuation">.</span>PooledByteBuffer$ClosedException<span class="token punctuation">:</span> Invalid bytebuf<span class="token punctuation">.</span> Already closed
<span class="token number">2023</span><span class="token operator">-</span><span class="token number">04</span><span class="token operator">-</span><span class="token number">13</span> <span class="token number">23</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token number">55</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token number">23.208</span> <span class="token number">11035</span><span class="token operator">-</span><span class="token number">11149</span> System<span class="token punctuation">.</span>err              com<span class="token punctuation">.</span>swing<span class="token punctuation">.</span>demo                  W  	<span class="token return-type class-name">at</span> com<span class="token punctuation">.</span>facebook<span class="token punctuation">.</span>imagepipeline<span class="token punctuation">.</span>memory<span class="token punctuation">.</span>NativePooledByteBuffer<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">ensureValid</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>NativePooledByteBuffer<span class="token punctuation">.</span>java<span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token number">103</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token number">2023</span><span class="token operator">-</span><span class="token number">04</span><span class="token operator">-</span><span class="token number">13</span> <span class="token number">23</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token number">55</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token number">23.208</span> <span class="token number">11035</span><span class="token operator">-</span><span class="token number">11149</span> System<span class="token punctuation">.</span>err              com<span class="token punctuation">.</span>swing<span class="token punctuation">.</span>demo                  W  	<span class="token return-type class-name">at</span> com<span class="token punctuation">.</span>facebook<span class="token punctuation">.</span>imagepipeline<span class="token punctuation">.</span>memory<span class="token punctuation">.</span>NativePooledByteBuffer<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">size</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>NativePooledByteBuffer<span class="token punctuation">.</span>java<span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token number">47</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token number">2023</span><span class="token operator">-</span><span class="token number">04</span><span class="token operator">-</span><span class="token number">13</span> <span class="token number">23</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token number">55</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token number">23.208</span> <span class="token number">11035</span><span class="token operator">-</span><span class="token number">11149</span> System<span class="token punctuation">.</span>err              com<span class="token punctuation">.</span>swing<span class="token punctuation">.</span>demo                  W  	<span class="token return-type class-name">at</span> com<span class="token punctuation">.</span>facebook<span class="token punctuation">.</span>imagepipeline<span class="token punctuation">.</span>memory<span class="token punctuation">.</span>PooledByteBufferInputStream<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">available</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>PooledByteBufferInputStream<span class="token punctuation">.</span>java<span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token number">50</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token number">2023</span><span class="token operator">-</span><span class="token number">04</span><span class="token operator">-</span><span class="token number">13</span> <span class="token number">23</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token number">55</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token number">23.208</span> <span class="token number">11035</span><span class="token operator">-</span><span class="token number">11149</span> System<span class="token punctuation">.</span>err              com<span class="token punctuation">.</span>swing<span class="token punctuation">.</span>demo                  W  	<span class="token return-type class-name">at</span> org<span class="token punctuation">.</span>chromium<span class="token punctuation">.</span>components<span class="token punctuation">.</span>embedder_support<span class="token punctuation">.</span>util<span class="token punctuation">.</span>InputStreamUtil<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">available</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>chromium<span class="token operator">-</span>TrichromeWebViewGoogle6432<span class="token punctuation">.</span>aab<span class="token operator">-</span>stable<span class="token operator">-</span><span class="token number">556311634</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     然后Chromium出现Error
    </p>
    <h3>
     <a id="_49">
     </a>
     三、原因
    </h3>
    <p>
     在image拦截中，使用Fresco缓存方式，使用了可关闭的引用(CloseableReference)
    </p>
    <p>
     Fresco-CloseableReference
     <br/>
     <a href="https://www.fresco-cn.org/docs/closeable-references.html" rel="nofollow">
      https://www.fresco-cn.org/docs/closeable-references.html
     </a>
    </p>
    <p>
     <strong>
      使用CloseableReference需注意：
     </strong>
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      调用者拥有这个引用
     </li>
     <li>
      持有者在离开作用域之前，需要关闭引用
     </li>
     <li>
      不要自己释放资源！
     </li>
     <li>
      除了引用的持有者，闲杂人等不得关闭引用
     </li>
     <li>
      在赋值给变量前，先进行clone
     </li>
    </ol>
    <h3>
     <a id="_62">
     </a>
     四、解决
    </h3>
    <p>
     检查代码，发现原因5.在赋值给变量前，先进行clone
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-csharp"><span class="token class-name">PooledByteBuffer</span> buffer <span class="token operator">=</span> reference<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token keyword">get</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
改为
<span class="token class-name">PooledByteBuffer</span> buffer <span class="token operator">=</span> reference<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">clone</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token keyword">get</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <h3>
     <a id="_71">
     </a>
     五、总结
    </h3>
    <ol>
     <li>
      log中 Error报的是Chrom内核的问题
     </li>
     <li>
      需先定位是什么原因导致的
     </li>
     <li>
      查看log中error往前看
     </li>
    </ol>
    <h3>
     <a id="_77">
     </a>
     六、日志整理
    </h3>

    <h3>
     <a id="Fatal_signal__291">
     </a>
     七、Fatal signal 错误
    </h3>
    <p>
     “Fatal signal” 是Android的一种闪退情况，表示出现了严重错误而导致应用程序被迫终止。这可能是由于多种原因造成的，下面是几种常见的 “Fatal signal” 错误情况：
    </p>
    <p>
     内存不足：当应用程序使用的内存超出了设备可用内存，并且无法释放内存时，可能会导致 “Fatal signal” 错误。
    </p>
    <p>
     代码逻辑错误：例如访问 null 引用变量、数组越界访问、类型转换错误等，都有可能导致 “Fatal signal” 错误。
    </p>
    <p>
     硬件相关：例如使用不兼容或不稳定的硬件设备、驱动程序、系统库等，也可能会导致 “Fatal signal” 错误。
    </p>
    <p>
     系统异常：例如设备磁盘故障、操作系统升级失败等，都有可能导致 “Fatal signal” 错误。
    </p>
    <p>
     第三方库相关：例如使用的第三方库出现了内部错误、版本不兼容等情况，也可能导致 “Fatal signal” 错误。
    </p>
    <p>
     总之， “Fatal signal” 错误很难确定具体的原因，因为它们可能是由多种因素造成的。我们需要详细了解日志中的错误信息，逐步尝试解决问题。一般情况下，可以通过查看应用程序的崩溃日志、设备日志、代码调试来解决这些问题。
    </p>
    <h3>
     <a id="_306">
     </a>
     八、写在最后
    </h3>
    <p>
